- **PLO_formula_validation_en.md**
  - HOW TO VERIFY THAT A PLO FORMULA WORKS [1]
  - Practical Validation Guide [2]
  - STEP 1: EXACT NUMERICAL VERIFICATION [6]
  - **Objective:** Confirm that it reproduces the experimental value [8]
  - Example: m_H = 5×41×61 / 1000 [13]
  - STEP 2: PRIME VERIFICATION [31]
  - **Objective:** Confirm that all factors are valid primes [33]
  - STEP 3: PHYSICAL COMPATIBILITY VERIFICATION [53]
  - **Objective:** Confirm that the T^k levels participate in the phenomenon [55]
  - STEP 4: BOUNDARY CONDITIONS VERIFICATION [79]
  - **Objective:** Confirm that the BCs are compatible [81]
  - STEP 5: ORDER OF MAGNITUDE VERIFICATION [102]
  - **Objective:** Confirm that the base (10^n) is appropriate [104]
  - STEP 6: UNIQUENESS VERIFICATION (OPTIONAL) [124]
  - **Objective:** Confirm that no other equally valid factorization exists [126]
  - STEP 7: CROSS-VERIFICATION (ADVANCED) [149]
  - **Objective:** Confirm coherence with related constants [151]
  - SUMMARY: VALIDATION CHECKLIST [176]
  - EXAMPLES OF VERIFIED FORMULAS [190]
  - **✓ VALID: m_u = 2³×3³ / 10⁵** [192]
  - **✓ VALID: Ω_Λ = 83² / 10⁴** [208]
  - **⚠️ WEAK: R_∞ (Rydberg) requires prime 52237** [224]
  - PROBLEMATIC CASES [240]

  - 8. SIGNIFICADO DE π EN ArXe [1121]
  - 8.1 Regla General [1123]
  - 8.2 Qué Nos Dice la Presencia de π [1128]
  - 1. Acoplamiento con Mediación Continua [1130]
  - Ejemplo: αₛ = 3π/(7×11) [1132]
  - 3 = grados de libertad temporales [1133]
  - π = ambigüedad de fase en mediación gluónica [1134]
  - 7×11 = estructura color-EM [1135]
  - 2. Excitación en Espacio Interno [1139]
  - Ejemplo: m_μ/m_e = 3⁴ + 40π + 2/19 [1141]
  - 40π = 8×5×π [1142]
  - 8 = octantes (2³) [1143]
  - 5 = curvatura (nivel T⁻²) [1144]
  - π = exploración de dimensiones ternarias internas [1145]
  - 3. Mezcla con Rotaciones Complejas [1149]
  - Ejemplo: θ₁₃ = 2π/(5×17×19) [1151]
  - 2π = ciclo completo de rotación [1152]
  - 5,17,19 = niveles de curvatura, hiper y materia oscura [1153]
  - 4. Propagación Isotrópica [1157]
  - Ejemplo: α⁻¹(∞) = 4π×11 [1159]
  - 4π = integral angular sobre esfera 3D [1160]
  - 11 = estructura EM pura [1161]
  - 8.3 Qué Nos Dice la Ausencia de π [1165]
  - 1. Estructura Discreta Pura [1167]
  - Ejemplo: sin²θ_w = 3/13 [1169]
  - Solo razón de primos [1170]
  - Sin ambigüedad de fase continua [1171]
  - 2. Combinación Lineal de Niveles [1175]
  - Ejemplo: α⁻¹ = 11² - 7² + 5×13 [1177]
  - Suma y resta de estructuras discretas [1178]
  - No hay mediación con grados libertad continuos [1179]
  - 3. Acoplamiento Directo Sin Fase [1183]
  - Ejemplo: Ω_Λ = (7×2×7)/(11×13) [1185]
  - Solo productos y cocientes de primos [1186]
  - 4. Propiedades Intrínsecas de Partícula [1190]
  - Ejemplo: Masa del Higgs [1192]
  - v × √(3/13) × (1 + 1/17) [1193]
  - Corrección discreta de nivel T⁻⁸ [1194]
